<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

Bianca must hide her supernatural heritage or risk certain death at its hands. But when Black Cross captures her friend—the vampire Balthazar—hiding is no longer an option. Soon Bianca and Lucas are on the run again, pursued not only by Black Cross, but by the powerful leaders of Evernight. Yet no matter how far they travel, Bianca can't escape her destiny. Bianca has always believed their love could survive anything... but can it survive what's to come?</span>

<div id="review_107251216" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/107251216" />
    <a title="Michael" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2638828-michael"><img alt="Michael" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590292807p2/2638828.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/107251216?book_show_action=true">Jun 15, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michael" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michael" href="/user/show/2638828-michael">Michael</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2638828-michael?shelf=judge-me">judge-me</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer107251216" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14670694599043349065"><b>6/16:</b><br/>Okay, I'm not even half way through this book, but I <i>had</i> to write a little something about how I felt so far. Basically, Bianca and Lucas are the most idiotic and annoying couple I've ever had the misfortune of reading about. And Bianca is probably the worst heroine in a novel. Ever. Okay, so her best friend (and almost lover) is in the next room being tortured. Lucas, the biggest douche-bag in life, is jealous because she is worried about what might happen to her friend. And then Bianca go</span>
  <span id="freeText14670694599043349065" style="display:none"><b>6/16:</b><br />Okay, I'm not even half way through this book, but I <i>had</i> to write a little something about how I felt so far. Basically, Bianca and Lucas are the most idiotic and annoying couple I've ever had the misfortune of reading about. And Bianca is probably the worst heroine in a novel. Ever. Okay, so her best friend (and almost lover) is in the next room being tortured. Lucas, the biggest douche-bag in life, is jealous because she is worried about what might happen to her friend. And then Bianca goes off with things like, "Oh Lucas, forgive me! Balthazar means nothing to me! You're the only one!" Seriously?<br /><br />Gah, this book is pissing me off.<br /><br />************************************************************************<br /><br /><b>6/18:</b><br />I finished it. And I must admit, it did get a little better. A <i>little</i>.<br /><br />I still hate Bianca and Lucas with a burning passion. Especially Bianca. She has got to be the most self-centered heroine in the history of literature. Almost all the hardships in this book are caused by the fact that Bianca cannot stand to leave her beloved Lucas. Almost half the book is Bianca talking about how madly in love she is with him and how perfect he is. Seriously, give me a break. Bianca says "Lucas" more in this book than Rose says "Jack" in <i>Titanic</i>. And seriously Claudia Gray (if that <i>is</i> your real name...) stop comparing Bianca and Lucas to Romeo and Juliet. For the love of God, no matter how much you want them to be, they will never be Romeo and Juliet.<br /><br />However, the plot saves this book from getting less than two stars. I've never had any doubts that Claudia Gray can spin an interesting storyline. Charity is interesting enough as an antagonist. And the part with the diving board was simple, but chilling nonetheless. The events that happen in the end are interesting as well, and should lead in to an interesting conclusion to the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14670694599043349065" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_95007590" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/95007590" />
    <a title="Gemma" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2279838-gemma"><img alt="Gemma" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1251085146p2/2279838.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/95007590?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gemma" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gemma" href="/user/show/2279838-gemma">Gemma</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780061981494" href="/book/show/7779805-hourglass">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2279838-gemma?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer95007590" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6507953839088401678">Ah, Evernight. No matter how much it tries, it always reminds me of a poor man's version of Vampire Academy. You know, the whole 'girl at a boarding school for vamps who falls for a stake wielding hot guy' thing. I hate comparing series; it's hard to write original YA nowadays, and it's near impossible to write a book without someone accusing you of stealing something from somebody else.<br/>When I began reading Hourglass, I realised all of the actions took place away from the school. I was a little </span>
  <span id="freeText6507953839088401678" style="display:none">Ah, Evernight. No matter how much it tries, it always reminds me of a poor man's version of Vampire Academy. You know, the whole 'girl at a boarding school for vamps who falls for a stake wielding hot guy' thing. I hate comparing series; it's hard to write original YA nowadays, and it's near impossible to write a book without someone accusing you of stealing something from somebody else.<br />When I began reading Hourglass, I realised all of the actions took place away from the school. I was a little sceptical, but hopeful this would distance the two series from each other.<br /><br />Once Bianca &amp; Lucas get away from the vamp vigilantes (finally), I was looking forward to some more original material. If they weren't going to return to Evernight, surely <i>something</i> big and dramatic would have to happen to keep the story going, right? So I waited. And waited. And waited some more. And about three quarters of the way in, I accepted that in fact, nothing particularly big and exciting was going to happen. Until I got to the ending. I'm sure this was meant to make me gasp in shock and excitement, but my gasp was caused by entirely different emotions. All I could really think was, 'But Ms Gray, you were doing so well!' Because when I read those final lines, my thoughts immediately went to the ending of said similar series, and I felt disappointed. I think that Evernight has the potential to be, and often is, a pretty original series, and I feel bad when I compare it to other series, mostly VA. But if there's going to be so many parallels between the two, usually one is found to be better, which undermines the other.<br /><br />Some people will probably disagree with me saying not much happens in Hourglass. Sure, revelations are made, particularly with Bianca &amp; her heritage, and other stuff crops up along the way. But most of said stuff was pretty predictable, and I ended up playing a waiting game through most of the book, wondering when the characters were going to figure out things that were right under their noses.<br />Most of the middle of the book comprises of Bianca &amp; Lucas drifting around, doing basically nothing. This down time seemed perfect for character development, something I've always felt is sorely lacking in Evernight. No matter how much the author tries, I've never felt connected to Bianca &amp; Lucas, which is pretty unforgivable considering they're the main characters. The series is written in first person, yet Bianca still remains a somewhat vague figure in my mind. I'm not sure if it's just because they're two dimensional, or whether it all harks back to me reading the first book and only being told halfway through that Bianca was in fact a vamp. I found this pretty ridiculous, considering I was supposed to be in her head and she'd conveniently forgot to mention her species; this subsequently made me see her as quite dim, and the author as amateurish.<br />Since most of this series revolves around the Romeo &amp; Juliet relationship between B &amp; L, my inability to really care about them is a huge blow to my ability to get into the series. They act more like two immature teens with a silly infatuation than two people deeply in love, and this usually results in me feeling pretty unsympathetic when something goes awry for them.<br />Saying that, I felt like I understood the characters a little better after Hourglass, Lucas especially, but it was all too little too late.<br /><br />I've heard Claudia Gray is writing a spin off series featuring the lovely Balthazar, who pops up briefly here to get tortured by Lucas's slap happy buddies. Despite my reservations about Evernight, I do quite like Balthazar - he seems more complex than others, and his sister issues are quite bizarre but interesting at the same time.<br />I'm hoping Claudia Gray won't do a number on him and turn him into a vapid pretty boy who is oblivious to the fact that his sister is totally insane, something that I suspect wouldn't be too hard to do, but I'll read it anyways.<br /><br />Probably the most shocking thing in Hourglass was that B &amp; L finally 'do it'. I say 'shocking' not because I have delicate sensibilities, more because after three books and more than enough moaning about restraint I'd just assumed it was going to be used as a crappy dramatic device to keep us reading (hello, Twilight). So I was pretty surprised Gray actually took the plunge, and applauded her development of the characters' relationship. However, after reading the ending, it became quite clear why this development had been made - something tells me Bianca &amp; Lucas won't be indulging themselves any time soon in their present conditions... :L<br /><br />I think I'll read the next book, if only to see how the hell Gray is going to sort out the mess the characters ended up in. But I'll be missing the excitement I had when I began Hourglass, and replacing it with a somewhat unhealthy dose of cynicism. Depressing, I know, but if this series doesn't clean up its act, I won't be reading it at all (:<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6507953839088401678" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_65788412" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/65788412" />
    <a title="Natalie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1969199-natalie"><img alt="Natalie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1427062916p2/1969199.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/65788412?book_show_action=true">Aug 01, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalie" href="/user/show/1969199-natalie">Natalie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer65788412" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9195037297224174089">I'm going to start off by saying that Hourglass is by far the best book in the series so far. While I definitely enjoyed Evernight and Stargazer, Hourglass surpassed the first two books in the series by leaps and bounds. If you stick around, I'm going to try to explain why.<br/><br/>First of all, the characters are much more complex. While this might be because of the background and development established by the first two books, Claudia Gray definitely showed what she can do with a pen in Hourglass. The </span>
  <span id="freeText9195037297224174089" style="display:none">I'm going to start off by saying that Hourglass is by far the best book in the series so far. While I definitely enjoyed Evernight and Stargazer, Hourglass surpassed the first two books in the series by leaps and bounds. If you stick around, I'm going to try to explain why.<br /><br />First of all, the characters are much more complex. While this might be because of the background and development established by the first two books, Claudia Gray definitely showed what she can do with a pen in Hourglass. The main characters are faced with even more difficult decisions, and they don't always make the choices you'd expect them to. I've always loved it when an author manages to throw me for a loop, and this happened a few times in this book.<br /><br />Second, the secondary characters were more fleshed out. We get to see more of Vic, Dana, Raquel, and Ranulf--including some things that I didn't see coming. For those of you who read this blog regularly, you know that for me, characters make the book, and in Hourglass, the loveable lead characters of Bianca and Lucas are supported by a cast of complex, well-developed minor characters.<br /><br />Furthermore, the entire book was emotionally charged. Anger, happiness, fear, grief, confusion--pretty much every emotion you could imagine was somehow included. I even shed a tear during one scene, and that's rare coming from me. The emotions were real, and they helped me to connect to the characters and identify with their situation, which is important in a series that focuses on the supernatural.<br /><br />Finally, I was impressed with where Gray took the series. After Stargazer, I was expecting to get shorted out on the wraith problem, by which I mean that I thought we'd get a kind of "wimpy" resolution. I've found that, in many series, other supernatural creatures are brought into the books just to make them more action-driven. I was expecting this to happen in Hourglass, but I was happily proven wrong.<br /><br />I don't know what I'm going to do waiting for the fourth book. The ending of Hourglass was awesome, but it left the characters in such a predicament that I'm wanting to beat down the author's door and demand the manuscript for the fourth book.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9195037297224174089" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Arlene" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene"><img alt="Arlene" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1347048609p2/1746727.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/62628966?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arlene" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arlene" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene">Arlene</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=read-2010">read-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=ya-paranormal">ya-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=ghosts">ghosts</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer62628966" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12669321849497607643">Claudia Gray has outdone herself with Hourglass. This book is the best of the series… BY FAR!! The twists, turns, struggles and climactic ending kept me riveted the entire time! All I have to say is (1) What an ending!! (2) When is Afterlife coming out?! and (3) I.CAN’T.WAIT!!! Wow… Just wow!<br/><br/>In this book Bianca and Lucas are together and trying to find an escape from the Black Cross Vampire Hunters before they figure out what Bianca truly is or isn’t for that matter. Their time together is since</span>
  <span id="freeText12669321849497607643" style="display:none">Claudia Gray has outdone herself with Hourglass. This book is the best of the series… BY FAR!! The twists, turns, struggles and climactic ending kept me riveted the entire time! All I have to say is (1) What an ending!! (2) When is Afterlife coming out?! and (3) I.CAN’T.WAIT!!! Wow… Just wow!<br /><br />In this book Bianca and Lucas are together and trying to find an escape from the Black Cross Vampire Hunters before they figure out what Bianca truly is or isn’t for that matter. Their time together is sincere, genuine and emotional. In Stargazer, I was a firm believer that Balthazar was the right choice for Bianca, but now Hourglass has me completely confused because Lucas is just perfect for her. This is truly the epic of all love triangles, even though we know who Bianca chooses, as a reader my heart went out to both.<br /><br />That last part of the book astonished me! Without giving it away, I never, NEVER saw that coming! I’m glad I didn’t read the last chapter of the book… OH! Warning, DO NOT read ahead, stay away from the last chapter! I did not expect that at all. Well, maybe I should have because we all know from the first book, Evernight, that Gray is capable of delivering plot twists that make your head spin.<br /><br />Great book, where the series continues to get better and better as it progresses. Hourglass is truly a book worth reading. A MUST.READ.NOW book. <br /></span>

          </span>

<div id="review_56808587" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/56808587" />
    <a title="Crystal" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2250501-crystal"><img alt="Crystal" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378941415p2/2250501.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/56808587?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Crystal" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Crystal" href="/user/show/2250501-crystal">Crystal</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2250501-crystal?shelf=2010">2010</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer56808587" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8067620260070874174">This book was my favorite in the series thus far. Gray throws in so many surprises that I am really chomping at the bit to get the next one! The story takes off where Stargazer left us with Bianca leaving Evernight with Lucas and his Black Cross family. Their biggest fear, they think, is that Bianca will be discovered for what she truly is, a vampire, but when you get to the final few chapters you will find out that they haven't even begun to realize what could possibly go wrong. I don't want to</span>
  <span id="freeText8067620260070874174" style="display:none">This book was my favorite in the series thus far. Gray throws in so many surprises that I am really chomping at the bit to get the next one! The story takes off where Stargazer left us with Bianca leaving Evernight with Lucas and his Black Cross family. Their biggest fear, they think, is that Bianca will be discovered for what she truly is, a vampire, but when you get to the final few chapters you will find out that they haven't even begun to realize what could possibly go wrong. I don't want to spoil it for anybody but the twists and turns that Gray develops are very unexpected at least to me and I am amazed that she had the strength to put her characters through so much. I give her big props for pushing her writing. Is Afterlife here yet??? </span>
  <a data-text-id="8067620260070874174" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_92837174" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/92837174" />
    <a title="Karyn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2236276-karyn"><img alt="Karyn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1333554205p2/2236276.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/92837174?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karyn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karyn" href="/user/show/2236276-karyn">Karyn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer92837174&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer92837174" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9358460244113548540">OMG! I was blown away. Completey caught off guard with this story. Claudia Gray took me on an emotional rollercoaster that had me petrified, elated, joyous, and utterly destroyed. I thought the Hunger Games were intense, but that was a walk in the park in comparison. Top 3 stories that I have ever read. My only concern is that the final book won't have the same intensity. March 2011 is too far away!<br/><br/>Summary<br/>The story starts with Bianca, Lucas, and Raquel with the Black Cross. The ask them to join </span>
  <span id="freeText9358460244113548540" style="display:none">OMG! I was blown away. Completey caught off guard with this story. Claudia Gray took me on an emotional rollercoaster that had me petrified, elated, joyous, and utterly destroyed. I thought the Hunger Games were intense, but that was a walk in the park in comparison. Top 3 stories that I have ever read. My only concern is that the final book won't have the same intensity. March 2011 is too far away!<br /><br />Summary<br />The story starts with Bianca, Lucas, and Raquel with the Black Cross. The ask them to join and Bianca is trapped into a yes. Raquel embraces her new membership and ability to fight back. The cell moves to NY for safety. There, they have to train hard and Bianca is often left hungry. In desparation, Lucas begs Bianca to drink from him and she agrees. This causes more changes in Bianca where she is now light headed and Lucas is more sensitive.<br /><br />During a patrol, Bianca sneeks off and emails her parents that she is fine. This leaves an electronic trail for Ms. Bethany which leads to an attack on the NYC Black Cross cell. Seven humans die - Eduardo is killed by Ms. Bethany. She also tells Bianca that she has to make a choice to be a vampire soon. Biance tells her that she will never choose to be a vampire. The cell retreats back to the river with a hostage - BALTHAZAR! They torture him for information, really torture, but Bianca and Lucas devise a ruse and free him to Chinatown.<br /><br />A few days later, Biance and Lucas are in the old hideout looking for their things when Dana and Raquel see Bianca drinking a packet of blood. Lucas explains everything and they promise to keep their secret. That night they are grabbed by the head of Black Cross who now knows the truth. They try to torture Bianca with pure holy water, but Lucas blocks getting burned himself. This makes him an enemy in their eyes and they decide to take Lucas and Bianca away to be tested by professors. Dana slips Lucas the handcuff keys and they escape. Although Raquel gave them up, Dana still loves Lucas as a brother. FYI - Dana and Raquel are a couple.<br /><br />Bianca and Lucas go to Chinatown to get money from Balthazar for their escape then head to Philadelphia. They get a hotel and then consumate their love. The next plan was to get in contact with Vic who lives in town. They meet up with Vic and Ranulf and turns out the Vic has known about the vampires all along. He gives Bianca and Lucas the keys to his house while he is in Tuscany with his parents and Ranulf.<br /><br />Lucas gets a job at a chop shop while Bianca tries to be a waitress. Her dizzy spells are gettign worse and she is no longer hungry. For her 18th birthday, Lucas takes Bianca to the Franklin Institute for the planetarium. He gives her a coral bracelet that becomes useful later. On their way home, they get surrounded by Charity's tribe and taken back to an abandoned pool. Charity wants a vampire family so she threatens Lucas' life to persuade Bianca to become a vampire. The wraiths come and save her and Lucas - "She is not yours. She is ours."<br /><br />Bianca is clearly dying. Lucas is there with her and offers his life so that she can live as a vampire. He only asks that Bianca kill him afterward so that he will not be a vampire. She refuses and dies, but not really since she becomes a wraith. Balthazar and Lucas bury her and then set out on a mission to capture Charity. Meanwhile, Bianca meets the wraith who has been haunting her, Maxie. She tells Bianca that the wraiths need her because she is pure and gives them energy. Maxie also shows her how to use her powers, specifically how to use the bracelet to have a body again.<br /><br />Vic and Ranulf come back after receiving Lucas' letter that Bianca is sick. Ranulf as a hard time working with a wraith since vampires and wraiths have been enemies. All three go to help Balthazar and Lucas. When they get there, Lucas is battling Charity and has LOST! She bit into him and drained him until he was dead. The story ends with Lucas in Bianca's lap, and Balthazar, Vic and Ranulf surrounding them. Lucas will become a vampire and Bianca blames Balthazar for not seeing how crazy his sister is and for taking Lucas on the mission to capture her. WOW!<br /><br />Characters - Black Cross<br /><br />Lucas<br /><br />Kate - Lucas' mom who tortures Balthazar during his capture. We don't know what happens to her or if she knows what has happened to Lucas. Will she be able to kill her son if it came to it?<br /><br />Eduardo - Kate's husband and real hard ass on Lucas. He takes Lucas' money preventing them from escaping sooner rather than later. During the raid by the vampires, he is killed by Ms. Bethany.<br /><br />Dana - Lucas' surrogate sister and best friend. They have been a part of the same cell since they were 12. She helps them escape and is in a relationship with Raquel.<br /><br />Raquel - Bianca's roommate who came with during the flee from the Evernight raid. She is extremely happy to be a member of Black Cross and wants revenge on all wraiths for the tortures that she has endured and the lies from the vampires.<br /><br />Eliza - head of the NYC Black Cross cell. Vicious killer.<br /><br />Milos - member of the NYC Black Cross cell.<br /><br /><br />Characters - Vampires<br /><br />Bianca's parents - not in this novel. Bianca is still mad at them so she doesn't talk to them. She does send a letter to them when she dies.<br /><br />Ms. Bethany - she is vicious and dangerous. Still don't know her plans.<br /><br />Balthazar - still clearly cares for Bianca and tries to save her from Black Cross when he gets captured. He is the first to arrive after her death and helps bury her. His greatest character flaw is his blind love for others. He does not see the evil in his sister or that Bianca will never be available. He is such a great character that he lose sight of this.<br /><br />Ranulf - LOVE HIM! Great character. He is one of the oldest vampires and has the toughest time adjusting to time. Vic takes him under his wing and they seem to become really good friends. Deadly warrior.<br /><br />Vic - not a vampire, but so loveable and funny. Has to one of the coolest, smartest, genuinely nicest characters ever.<br /><br />Questions for the next novel - <br />1. There seems to be 2 wars going on; Vampires vs. Black Cross and Vampires vs. Wraiths. How does that resolve? Ms. Bethany seems to be a key player, but I can't seem to foreshadow an ending.<br />2. LUCAS IS A VAMPIRE - he never wanted to be. Will he choose to end his life and then become a wraith so that he and Bianca can spend eternity together?<br />3. Black Cross? There has to be some form of confrontation between them and Lucas.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9358460244113548540" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2760618-gio?shelf=bad">bad</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer97894757" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer840401882070755694">severely disappointing read..... I thought the first book was ok and wasnt really interested in continuing the series however I was bored and read Stargazer which interestingly enough spiked my interest. Butttttttttt with Hourglass I am afraid to say, Claudia took 3 steps back<br/><br/>In all honesty I find lucas's character to be very boring and uninteresting so I found it hard for me to root for them to be together because I really don't understand what Bianca saw in him. However in Hourglass I could no</span>
  <span id="freeText840401882070755694" style="display:none">severely disappointing read..... I thought the first book was ok and wasnt really interested in continuing the series however I was bored and read Stargazer which interestingly enough spiked my interest. Butttttttttt with Hourglass I am afraid to say, Claudia took 3 steps back<br /><br />In all honesty I find lucas's character to be very boring and uninteresting so I found it hard for me to root for them to be together because I really don't understand what Bianca saw in him. However in Hourglass I could not stand Bianca either she became to me one those characters that are too stupid to live. She.... no both of them.....are very stupid and immature. Bianca for some reason stupidly and blindly trusts Lucas to take care of her when he doesn't want to go to college and can't even work with the vampire hunters anymore and his big plan is for them to work at fast food restaurants. Wow Bianca and Lucas! And how could they not figure out that when she was becoming ill that it has nothing to do with the fact that she is part wraith ughhh. And Lucas what the fuck, if he really loved Bianca why would he not lower his pride and call Biancas parents for help when she needed because obviously he didn't know what the fuck was going on with her.<br /><br />And I was upset by the fact that Claudia didn't develop her characters more in this book especially since they really didn't do anything the entire novel. I don't really feel connected to Bianca in Hourglass at all because the only thing I wanted to do was literally slap some sense into her. And with Lucas I never did find that many qualities that I like about him. To me he was just a silly infatuated boy ruled by his hormones and I felt like neither Bianca or Lucas spent enough time together to truly like each other.<br /><br />But anyway needless to say I won't be reading anymore books on this series.</span>

Lucas and Bianca have had there love tested in so many different ways, and yet there love is so strong. It's a beautiful thing and I simply adore them! They both have grown up and you can feel that in Hourglass, there romance is not only tender but hot and I can't help but smile when I think of them!<br />But we don't just get some romance in this book, there are a lot of surprises and twists in this book. <div id="review_993287336" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/993287336" />
    <a title="Nicole - Too Weird To Live, Too Rare To Die-" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21398856-nicole---too-weird-to-live-too-rare-to-die-"><img alt="Nicole - Too Weird To Live, Too Rare To Die-" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587944547p2/21398856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/993287336?book_show_action=true">Jul 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nicole - Too Weird To Live, Too Rare To Die-" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nicole - Too Weird To Live, Too Rare To Die-" href="/user/show/21398856-nicole---too-weird-to-live-too-rare-to-die-">Nicole - Too Weird To Live, Too Rare To Die-</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780061284489" href="/book/show/6421587-hourglass">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21398856-nicole---too-weird-to-live-too-rare-to-die-?shelf=completed-books">completed-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer993287336" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8920689227770925181">Bianca will risk everything to be with Lucas.<br/><br/>After escaping from Evernight, the vampire boarding school where they met, Bianca and Lucas seek refuge with Black Cross, an elite group of vampire hunters. Bianca must hide her supernatural heritage or risk certain death at its hands. But when Black Cross captures her friend—the vampire Balthazar—all her secrets threaten to come out.<br/><br/>Soon, Bianca and Lucas are on the run, pursued not only by Black Cross, but by the powerful vampires of Evernight. Yet </span>
  <span id="freeText8920689227770925181" style="display:none">Bianca will risk everything to be with Lucas.<br /><br />After escaping from Evernight, the vampire boarding school where they met, Bianca and Lucas seek refuge with Black Cross, an elite group of vampire hunters. Bianca must hide her supernatural heritage or risk certain death at its hands. But when Black Cross captures her friend—the vampire Balthazar—all her secrets threaten to come out.<br /><br />Soon, Bianca and Lucas are on the run, pursued not only by Black Cross, but by the powerful vampires of Evernight. Yet no matter how far they run, Bianca can't escape her destiny. Bianca and Lucas have always believed their love could survive anything—but can it survive what's to come?<br /><br /><b> 5 the roles have switched now stars </b><br /><br />“This could be our greatest nightmare. But maybe, instead this would be our only hope of salvation.” <br /><br /> I was not prepared for the plot twist at the end of this book, which shocked me the most because you expect them to be what their originally going to be like Bianca as a vampire and Lucas maybe changed or stayed human because he didn't want to be a vampire but no they switched where Lucas is the vampire and Bianca is a ghost who both have destiny tied with each other and to see if they can last through this and what will happen in the second last book in the series but after that we have a book in Balthazar Point of view which I'm excited about because he was my favorite character. <br /><br />This story surprised me because i thought it would be like the other ones and be a little bit better, but this one actually surprised me because of all the action throughout the book and how many problems they had to deal with just the two of them but what broke my hear the most is when Lucas saw Bianca die, that hurt so much because he loved her so much and too see her sick like that practically broke my heart and just made it super emotional too read and too feel how the characters felt during that scene made me feel different towards them, than previously in the different books I wonder how this is going to all play out in the last book and how there going to fix this problem.<br /><br />There is also where we have to deal with a new villain and the same one trying to figure out what they want with Bianca, Lucas and maybe even Balthazar, but also left out what will happen with the other characters if they find out what happens to those three or even when Bianca parents find out she died to see if they will do anything to bring their child back and make her change than into a vampire because they never wanted their child to leave them after they did everything they could to get Bianca and now how are they going to react if they find out she is dead. Also what is Ms. Bethany going to do cause she wants to use the wraiths for her own personal gain or does she have something else in mind involving these wraiths?. What is their major plan also involving Bianca because Massie said she is the purest wraith and can help with a major plan that they have. <br /><br />This book was very interesting to see the two different worlds collide in the most epic love story between a vampire and human which the roles have switched and how that going to work with everything else and how will old enemy take place in their new lives. we find out in the last book in the Evernight series. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8920689227770925181" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_93485980" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/93485980" />
    <a title="Bex" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3283584-bex"><img alt="Bex" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1453031340p2/3283584.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/93485980?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bex" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bex" href="/user/show/3283584-bex">Bex</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3283584-bex?shelf=own">own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer93485980" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer422006906575776627">I love to be taken by surprise. It doesn't happen all that often, so I really relish the times that it does. I have to admit I was a little apprehensive when I started Hourglass. The plot was a little slow moving, there wasn't that tension or anticipation between Bianca and Lucas.. will they be together, will they not be together? I think that helped the first two novels move along a little more quickly. <br/><br/>The last quarter of the novel is really what did it for me. I wanted to read the book becaus</span>
  <span id="freeText422006906575776627" style="display:none">I love to be taken by surprise. It doesn't happen all that often, so I really relish the times that it does. I have to admit I was a little apprehensive when I started Hourglass. The plot was a little slow moving, there wasn't that tension or anticipation between Bianca and Lucas.. will they be together, will they not be together? I think that helped the first two novels move along a little more quickly. <br /><br />The last quarter of the novel is really what did it for me. I wanted to read the book because I do enjoy the series, but had that last quarter not happened... I think my rating would have been a lot lower. Totally did not see it coming and I'm very curious as to what is going to happen next. <br /><br />So besides the plot another thing that bothers me is Bianca. I don't really like her. She kind of annoys me. A LOT. Her character is just so..... mature. And not in a good mature teen kind of way, but in a very worldly mature kind of way. Which isn't what her character is supposed to be at all. She isn't a vampire that has been around for centuries, she really is just a teenager. I mean what kind of teenager uses the word lover? As in being in bed with a lover....? Maybe it's just me, but her character just isn't consistent. BUT the real character behind my love for this series is Balthazar. Give me a piece of that! Love everything about this guy and he is in this novel plenty, which I of course lapped up like a kitten would a saucer of milk. Meow! Was that too much? I'm usually not a metaphor person, but hey I'm just in that mood. I will admit that Lucas did start to grow on me a little bit. He finally grew a backbone somewhere in there. <br /><br />Hourglass was a little steamier then the previous two novels as well! I'm a steamy fan though, so I enjoyed that part. And it was done tastefully too. Which is always nice, especially in young adult fiction. <br /><br />Gray has a very addicting writing style I think that is what kept me going despite the slowish plot and my annoyance of Bianca. I am really looking forward to the final installment: AFTERLIFE! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="422006906575776627" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7519540491054868498">I had a review all written out and then my Male-counter-part turned off the computer when I left it like a ninny, so now it's gone.<br/><br/>In short though, this book had an exceptionally unhealthy idea of relationships, including, but not limited to:<br/>+ Terrifying "he's going to yell at me when we get home" thoughts about her super-stud, personality void, hot-headed boyfriend, which were not in any way shown to be a bad thing.<br/>+ Endorsed "Die for each other" mentality after only a few <i>weeks</i> of dating.<br/>+ Con</span>
  <span id="freeText7519540491054868498" style="display:none">I had a review all written out and then my Male-counter-part turned off the computer when I left it like a ninny, so now it's gone.<br /><br />In short though, this book had an exceptionally unhealthy idea of relationships, including, but not limited to:<br />+ Terrifying "he's going to yell at me when we get home" thoughts about her super-stud, personality void, hot-headed boyfriend, which were not in any way shown to be a bad thing.<br />+ Endorsed "Die for each other" mentality after only a few <i>weeks</i> of dating.<br />+ Condescending acceptance of a LBGT friend like it was some sort of achievement not to freak out at their confession.<br />+ And "Please forgive them for trying to murder you, they'll regret it later" requests, which she considers ok.<br /><br />Our leading lady was the most infuriatingly useless female lead I have ever read.<br />Next to Bella Swan. <br />She does literally nothing but cry and faint for the entire book, until the last like, 80 pages, where she still doesn't do all that much by herself. That's not an exaggeration. I kept track, she doesn't do <i>anything</i>.<br />This book is obviously written for younger YA than me, but that's what makes it so scary. If girls are learning from these kind of books then they're receiving terrible messages about what a "protective" boyfriend is and how you should treat everyone you know once you get one. They're learning to think of themselves a fragile and incomplete without a partner and that that partner will just enable their uselessness.<br /><br />I disliked this book so much that I almost didn't cry when my cat chewed on the corner of the book when I left it on the table like a ninny.<br />Maybe I should learn a lesson about leaving things unattended.<br />So this book taught me something after all!<br /></span>

<div id="review_97030272" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/97030272" />
    <a title="Stef" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2307279-stef"><img alt="Stef" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540183443p2/2307279.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/97030272?book_show_action=true">Apr 04, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stef" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stef" href="/user/show/2307279-stef">Stef</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2307279-stef?shelf=paranormal-young-adult">paranormal-young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer97030272" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10161351491069393164">Star crossed lovers stuck in Paranormal Tug-a-War <br/><br/>**Third book in the series so its spoilers galore for the first two books.**<br/><br/>Bianca and Lucas are the star crossed lovers of the Evernight series. This love story that I’ve come to love has grown into something much more complex than any other Romeo and Juliet stylized story.<br/><br/>Hourglass takes off right where Stargazer left off. Bianca and her Evernight school room mate, Raquel have joined forces with the Black Cross. As we learned before, the Black </span>
  <span id="freeText10161351491069393164" style="display:none">Star crossed lovers stuck in Paranormal Tug-a-War <br /><br />**Third book in the series so its spoilers galore for the first two books.**<br /><br />Bianca and Lucas are the star crossed lovers of the Evernight series. This love story that I’ve come to love has grown into something much more complex than any other Romeo and Juliet stylized story.<br /><br />Hourglass takes off right where Stargazer left off. Bianca and her Evernight school room mate, Raquel have joined forces with the Black Cross. As we learned before, the Black Cross is a team of Vampire hunters and view all vampires to be the all the same cold blooded killers. In return the vampires think the same about them. The motto seems to be kill first, ask later. This bothers Bianca more than ever before now that she has her nose being rubbed in it, and is being trained to do the exact same thing to beings of her own kind. Bianca’s true identity is still hidden from everyone in the Black Cross and even from Raquel. With everyone having such black and white opinions on everything, Bianca stands no chance of ever being accepted for what and who she really is. On the bright side, Bianca and Lucas finally get to be together. Although with this new soldier life style they see less of each other than when they were sneaking around and separated by many miles instead of under the same roof. <br /><br />Their star crossed lover issues are far from over though. The vampires of Evernight, the wraiths, and Charity and her tribe are all after them with deadly force. People Bianca and Lucas may have trusted in the beginning will fail them at some point in the most surprising ways. With all the danger, there’s a natural magnetic sexual tension that burns hot and long between Bianca and Lucas. It makes you root for them every step of the way of their dramatic adventure. Even at the most heartbreaking times and when you think its impossible for them to be in the same place at the same time, hope stays alive. Hope drives their love and makes it burn stronger.<br /><br />I was frustrated at points of the book, mainly because you’re so wrapped up in Lucas and Bianca’s raw emotions. To balance it out you have the light hearted and charming Vic with his vampire sidekick, Ranulf. I think everyone could use a Vic in their lives. He sees in shades of gray instead of just black and white. He’s laid back and accepting of everything thrown his way and not everyone has such grace under pressure. <br /><br />Everything got very intense near the end and it really makes you beg for more. What a great read. This is a series in which you start out slow and you might be not all that impressed with the pace at the beginning, but you will not be the least disappointed if you keep reading. Its hitting its own level of greatness with each coming book. Great for all YA paranormal romance readers. Trust me, you’ll love it long time.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10161351491069393164" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780061284410" href="/book/show/6609636-hourglass">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1310688-kristi?shelf=signed-arcs">signed-arcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1310688-kristi?shelf=signed-books">signed-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1310688-kristi?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1310688-kristi?shelf=own-arc">own-arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer53869810" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7285532901976420539">I love to be taken by surprise. It doesn't happen all that often, so I really relish the times that it does. I have to admit I was a little apprehensive when I started Hourglass. The plot was a little slow moving, there wasn't that tension or anticipation between Bianca and Lucas.. will they be together, will they not be together? I think that helped the first two novels move along a little more quickly.<br/><br/>The last quarter of the novel is really what did it for me. I wanted to read the book because</span>
  <span id="freeText7285532901976420539" style="display:none">I love to be taken by surprise. It doesn't happen all that often, so I really relish the times that it does. I have to admit I was a little apprehensive when I started Hourglass. The plot was a little slow moving, there wasn't that tension or anticipation between Bianca and Lucas.. will they be together, will they not be together? I think that helped the first two novels move along a little more quickly.<br /><br />The last quarter of the novel is really what did it for me. I wanted to read the book because I do enjoy the series, but had that last quarter not happened... I think my rating would have been a lot lower. Totally did not see it coming and I'm very curious as to what is going to happen next.<br /><br />So besides the plot another thing that bothers me is Bianca. I don't really like her. She kind of annoys me. A LOT. Her character is just so..... mature. And not in a good mature teen kind of way, but in a very worldly mature kind of way. Which isn't what her character is supposed to be at all. She isn't a vampire that has been around for centuries, she really is just a teenager. I mean what kind of teenager uses the word lover? As in being in bed with a lover....? Maybe it's just me, but her character just isn't consistent. BUT the real character behind my love for this series is Balthazar. Give me a piece of that! Love everything about this guy and he is in this novel plenty, which I of course lapped up like a kitten would a saucer of milk. Meow! Was that too much? I'm usually not a metaphor person, but hey I'm just in that mood. I will admit that Lucas did start to grow on me a little bit. He finally grew a backbone somewhere in there.<br /><br />Hourglass was a little steamier then the previous two novels as well! I'm a steamy fan though, so I enjoyed that part. And it was done tastefully too. Which is always nice, especially in young adult fiction.<br /><br />Gray has a very addicting writing style I think that is what kept me going despite the slowish plot and my annoyance of Bianca. I am really looking forward to the final installment: AFTERLIFE!<br /><br />(I've also heard rumors of a Balthazar spin off... YES PLEASE!)</span>
  <a data-text-id="7285532901976420539" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer17546188033572542563">Holy smokes! What an ending... I didn't see any of that coming. I can't wait for the fourth book. Man, where is Claudia Gray going to takes us. <br/><br/>How to explain my three star rating though. Some of my reasoning comes from not only this book, but some other unfortunate reads lately. It seems the past few books have had less than mediocre leading ladies. More specifically, they have been overly naive and well, just plain stupid...<br/><br/>Then, there is the whole love-triangle thing. Oh how I hate them and t</span>
  <span id="freeText17546188033572542563" style="display:none">Holy smokes! What an ending... I didn't see any of that coming. I can't wait for the fourth book. Man, where is Claudia Gray going to takes us. <br /><br />How to explain my three star rating though. Some of my reasoning comes from not only this book, but some other unfortunate reads lately. It seems the past few books have had less than mediocre leading ladies. More specifically, they have been overly naive and well, just plain stupid...<br /><br />Then, there is the whole love-triangle thing. Oh how I hate them and this is my opinion of why. Usually, the mix is two guys in love with the same girl. The girl being in the middle acts all hopeless and moony. She also seems wishy-washy. Can't decide who she loves most. The decision always comes at the very end, after I'm ready to scream. Literally. <br /><br />On the other hand, there are the men. There is the supposed "true-love" and the other is the second-hand hopeless case, waiting in the wings. The "true-love" always sits by and watches as the girl and the wing-man act all love-dovey. Man, if that was me, I would say "see ya." I wouldn't stand by and watch the person I love hanging all over some one else or allow them to exchange romantic gestures. But hey, that's just me... <br /><br />Overall, I think the love-triangle has been over done, played out. Plus, the girl characters who are portrayed as clumsy halfwits need to have a make-over or something. Get some new material people... Hellooo!<br /><br />I read a lot of the same type books because I love them so much. But, there are those books that stand out for the awesomeness of their originality and the excellence of writing, and then there are the other books that ride on the coattails of the best...<br /><br />Books shouldn't be like a floor plan where you follow the pattern and just fill in different names and stuff. <br /><br />I'm not sure where that all came from...</span>
  <a data-text-id="17546188033572542563" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9001140305175768190">Just finished reading this book. <br/>I am so torn, I loved it and almost hated it!! Let me explain....<br/><br/>The book was amazing, I could not stop reading it. Once I started it I couldn't put it down, only to do things that had to be done. I have loved this series from the beginning. I loved the way Gray introduced the vampires, how Bianca found out what she was, or part of what she was, it was brilliant. I was caught up in the whirlwind of Lucas and Balthazar.<br/><br/>This book picked up right where the second on</span>
  <span id="freeText9001140305175768190" style="display:none">Just finished reading this book. <br />I am so torn, I loved it and almost hated it!! Let me explain....<br /><br />The book was amazing, I could not stop reading it. Once I started it I couldn't put it down, only to do things that had to be done. I have loved this series from the beginning. I loved the way Gray introduced the vampires, how Bianca found out what she was, or part of what she was, it was brilliant. I was caught up in the whirlwind of Lucas and Balthazar.<br /><br />This book picked up right where the second one finished. Bianca and Lucas are fighting to survive with the Black Cross, Bianca has to learn so much, and endure so much just to keep her true identity a secret. Lucas sacrifices so much for her, more so than I think he could imagine.<br /><br />The book was very emotional, had me in tears a lot. Had me gasping until I turned the page, and made me fall in love all of over again.<br /><br />The part that I hated, and hate is really too strong of a word. The part that shocked me, and had me wishing for something different was the ending. I was really surprised with the way she ended the book. Completely left me staring at the page screaming NO!!!!!!!!!!! it can not finish, I turned the pages and they were blank. I was devastated, now to wait until next year for Afterlife to come out, will be torture.<br /><br />I love Gray's writing style, I love her characters and the story is unique and exciting. I have a lot of strong emotions towards the characters. I am so anxious to see what happens next..<br />Great book, for me a huge shock at the end.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10934313777187966848">i had already heard that there was a cliffhanger ending, so i was somewhat prepared for it, but still, i can't believe what happened. i have so many questions and i can't even imagine how things will play out in the the next and final book.<br/><br/>thankfully my beloved balthazar is back, though tormented still. i can't put my finger on it, but he is such a likable character - always thinking of others and how to help others. lucas's intensity as well as his compassion was really well portrayed. i do wis</span>
  <span id="freeText10934313777187966848" style="display:none">i had already heard that there was a cliffhanger ending, so i was somewhat prepared for it, but still, i can't believe what happened. i have so many questions and i can't even imagine how things will play out in the the next and final book.<br /><br />thankfully my beloved balthazar is back, though tormented still. i can't put my finger on it, but he is such a likable character - always thinking of others and how to help others. lucas's intensity as well as his compassion was really well portrayed. i do wish that kate had more face time - she's good people. <br /><br />as for the rest of black cross and even the vampires, it seems like they're so focused on protecting and killing their enemy that they can't see past the exterior. their utter hatred, fear and stubborn ignorance actually make me think about race issues though i do not think this was the author's aim.<br /><br />when it comes down to it, despite the vampires and wraiths and black cross, this is a love story and quite a good one at that. lucas and bianca are deliciously in love and thus will do anything for each other. unfortunately we're left wondering what will happen in 'afterlife' since no ends have been tied up. there is so much information that we lack, since bianca herself doesn't know how things work exactly and i'm sure all questions will be answered in 'afterlife' but now i have to wait a year until it comes out...<br /><br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/97066652?book_show_action=true">Apr 04, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carie" href="/user/show/2187401-carie">Carie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer97066652" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10578382700127728779">I’m really not sure what I think about this book. I couldn’t put it down, just like the first two, but there were lots of things to irritate me. I was really irritated that the characters weren’t smarter—-especially Bianca. Why could she not see things that were very obvious to the reader!? Or make better decisions? I found Raquel and her rigidity incredibly irritating. I, again, found the lack of knowledge about Lucas to be irritating—-I would like more personal experiences/information about hi</span>
  <span id="freeText10578382700127728779" style="display:none">I’m really not sure what I think about this book. I couldn’t put it down, just like the first two, but there were lots of things to irritate me. I was really irritated that the characters weren’t smarter—-especially Bianca. Why could she not see things that were very obvious to the reader!? Or make better decisions? I found Raquel and her rigidity incredibly irritating. I, again, found the lack of knowledge about Lucas to be irritating—-I would like more personal experiences/information about him shared with Bianca or something to help me understand and know him better. I still feel more of a connection to Balthazar than to Lucas, and the lack of lots of Balthazar in this book was irritating! And, the state of Bianca at the end of the book, though predictable, was beyond irritating!!<br /><br />The last 100 or so pages of the book were excruciating and at one point I felt like closing the book for good; however, I persevered and was glad I did for the last few pages. The ending leaves lots of intriguing possibilities and new problems for the couple. So, I’m looking forward to the next installment.<br /><br />One thing (SPOILER): If Bianca knows how abhorrent Lucas would find his final predicament, why would she allow him to “wake up” in the morning?!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10578382700127728779" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer90188889" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10392077159801373362">This book puts the M in melodramatic. But the story and characters are so good and so strong that the melodrama doesn't ruin the story at all. This really kept me turning the pages because i just had to see what would happen next, and the ending. Oh, the ending. Gray gives us such a HUGE cliffhanger, i'm reaaaaaaaaaaally looking forward to the final book Afterlife. I really loved this book and i can't wait to see how Gray wraps it all up. I also love the characters, Bianca in particular. Her cha</span>
  <span id="freeText10392077159801373362" style="display:none">This book puts the M in melodramatic. But the story and characters are so good and so strong that the melodrama doesn't ruin the story at all. This really kept me turning the pages because i just had to see what would happen next, and the ending. Oh, the ending. Gray gives us such a HUGE cliffhanger, i'm reaaaaaaaaaaally looking forward to the final book Afterlife. I really loved this book and i can't wait to see how Gray wraps it all up. I also love the characters, Bianca in particular. Her character is very strong and she's not a wimp or a wuss and while she does love Lucas very deeply and abidingly, it's not obsessive and her world doesn't revolve around him. And Lucas is great too, he loves Bianca just as much as she loves him, but's he not obsessive either. All in all one of the best YA vampire romance novel series currently available and well worth reading. And a perfect Twilight antidote, because the whole series is way better than the Twilight saga, the writing is far better, the characters are far better and the plot is far better too.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7N3r8lWJPmdagZRUyb9b20iSrUK/yIw60V+el7yTMzDW+4Ig7tf3D/2qIDU+SlEEns1KinFFAl2KIdgmcdDBqg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('koJYGwubI6IiYaWADkCJHaFakslyQswZtxM781tyXwaopDHJsMXqyoVKEeH5tYPCdwV1AbzPQn7sbX1CljGtnA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer2383906837341763535">Claudia Gray is not my real name. I didn't choose a pseudonym because my real name is unpleasant (it isn't), because I'd always dreamed of calling myself this (I haven't) or even because I'm hiding from the remnants of that international diamond-smuggling cartel I smashed in 2003 (Interpol has taken care of them). In short, I took a pseudonym for no real reason whatsoever. Sometimes this is actual</span>
  <span id="freeText2383906837341763535" style="display:none">Claudia Gray is not my real name. I didn't choose a pseudonym because my real name is unpleasant (it isn't), because I'd always dreamed of calling myself this (I haven't) or even because I'm hiding from the remnants of that international diamond-smuggling cartel I smashed in 2003 (Interpol has taken care of them). In short, I took a pseudonym for no real reason whatsoever. Sometimes this is actually the best reason to do things.<br /><br />I live in New Orleans. So far, in life, I've been a disc jockey, a lawyer, a journalist and an extremely bad waitress, just to name a few. I especially like to spend time traveling, hiking, reading and listening to music. More than anything else, I enjoy writing. <br /></span>
